The room is not well soundproofed. You can hear everything going on next door. The air conditioner in the room was set to 30°C, but it didn't work and I woke up from the freezing cold in the middle of the night.
It took a little longer to take a shower in the bathroom, but it was all filled with water. The toilet is equipped for disabled people. I don’t know if this room is a special room. Anyway, it feels very bad. All the lights in the whole room were turned on, but it was also dim. I emphasized that what I was dealing with was the hotel's service, not a little girl. It was an issue of internal communication in the hotel and the staff's work flow. She causes problems and blames other people's problems. She does not have the qualities of a five-star hotel at all. She is a little girl with poor working ability. She is full of lies. msg:Beijing R&F Wanda Realm Hotel is located along the West Chang'an Avenue in Beijing, in Shijingshan District, with a superior geographical location, next to the most popular Wanda Plaza in Shijingshan, and very close to the Shijingshan District Government.
Wanda Realm (REALM) is a series second only to Wanda Ruihua (Reign) and Wanda Vista (Wanda Vista), but its positioning is higher than Jinhua and Meihua.
On the second floor of the hotel, there is a large-scale Pinzhen Chinese restaurant with private rooms of various sizes; on the third floor is the fitness center and swimming pool, which are open from morning to 11 pm, and table tennis facilities cost 40 yuan an hour; hotel weekends And holidays often undertake large-scale wedding banquets.
Some public welfare activities are often held in the hotel lobby on weekends, such as "Earth Hour", during which free small cakes will be provided to guests in the lobby, and free candies will also be provided to children.
I checked in on March 25, 2023. Generally speaking, the hotel meets the five-star standard. The service staff are warm and friendly, and the facilities are complete. The TV in the room can watch foreign channels such as CNN, CNA, HBO, Russia Today, etc. Overall, I am very satisfied. It's just that the parking lot is too small (the underground parking lot can't be used), and you have to wait in line to get a parking space on weekends. You can only use one parking ticket a day; there is no toilet next to the swimming pool. inconvenient.

Staying at the hotel is a bit too much, but today I don’t want to comment on the quality of the hotel. R&F Wanda is a five-star hotel, so the standard needn't be said much. It must be comfortable and reassuring in all aspects.
However, what I encountered tonight was shockingly moved and made me dreamy, haha.
I want to call the customer service front desk sister Yin Huan’s ultimate service——
1. By coincidence, I forgot to bring laundry detergent on this trip. At 11:30 in the evening, I took the liberty to call the front desk to see if there is any laundry detergent. "The laundry room is closed", and I am ready to give up.
2. Yin Huan went on to say that she wanted to find a way;
3. Then let me wait for a while, she briefly handed over the front desk work and went to the dormitory to get some laundry detergent for me;
4. Ask me if I would mind filling with mineral water bottles, "Of course I don't mind."
5. After a long time, knock on the door and send a small bottle of laundry detergent.
It's not a big deal, but something that could have been let go, the front desk girl is serious and thoughtful to ensure the needs of the residents, which really touched me!
At the moment I knocked on the door, I saw that R&F Wanda's customer service training was very in place, and the girl has been respectful, even if it is such a proactive service that can say "no", it still makes people feel like a spring breeze, adding a touch of pleasure to my Beijing trip!
It has been raining these few days, the air is fresh, and Wanyue’s service makes me cool!

msg:我從來沒見過這麼差的五星級酒店，不但設施差，而且服務差。
早餐廳的椅子把我的手指劃破，服務員向我道歉，説會送一盤水果到房間以表歉意，但最終沒有。CHECK OUT的時候前台服務員拍了我手機上的開票訊息，但開出來的發票地址卻是錯的。當我寄回發票要求重開，第二次開出來的發票地址改對了，金額卻又不對了，我不知道一家五星級酒店的服務是不是不帶腦子上班的，這種低級錯誤不停地犯而且沒有人來真誠地道歉。第二次的發票我寄回給酒店，11月11日酒店就簽收了，到目前11月16日為止我卻還沒收到酒店寄回給我的正確的發票。給客户造成了這麼**煩，還沒相關人員來跟蹤此事，這是一家五星級酒店該有的服務嗎？

info:Superior Deluxe Double Room
info:Stayed in October 2021
info:Other
info:2 Reviews
rating:3.2
posted:Posted October 11, 2021
msg:第一次住萬達嘉華這個品牌 設備設施離五星級酒店還是有很大差距的
1.床達不到五星標準 躺上去就直接感覺躺在了硬板彈簧床墊上
2.酒店的窗户漏風非常嚴重 如果住在高樓層 朝北的房間 風聲大的感覺就像住在馬路上
3. 衞生間遮擋簾的設計很迷 開關在衞生間裏面 簾子在衞生間外面 且放下簾子後外面看裏面看的一清二楚 建議有私密淋浴如廁需求的客人不要定大床房
4.服務倒是可以接受 半夜打電話説噪音太大 給安排了換房 換到低樓層 雖然房間面積小了些 但是確實聽不到風聲了 不過空調噪音很大 衹能關了空調 而且不知道為什麼酒店的床竟然不一樣 新房間的床明顯比樓上的軟了很多
----------------------------------------
